                cuisines: ['African', 'Alcohol', 'American', 'Asian', 'Bagels', 'Bakery', 'Barbecue', 'Beer', 'Breakfast & Brunch', 'Burgers', 'Canadian', 'Catering', 'Chicken', 'Chinese', 'Coffee/Tea', 'Delicatessen', 'Desserts', 'Diner', 'Donair', 'Ethiopian', 'European', 'Family Fare', 'Fast Food', 'Fish and Chips', 'French', 'Fusion', 'Gluten Free', 'Gluten Friendly', 'Greek', 'Halal', 'Haute Cuisine', 'Healthy', 'Homemade', 'Hot Dogs & Sausages', 'Ice Cream & Frozen Treats', 'Indian', 'International', 'Italian', 'Japanese', 'Korean', 'Liquor', 'Locally Sourced', 'Mediterranean', 'Mexican', 'Middle Eastern', 'Noodle Shop', 'Organic', 'Pasta', 'Pitas', 'Pizza', 'Pub Food', 'Restaurant Awards', 'Sandwiches & Subs', 'Seafood', 'Smoothies', 'Spirits', 'Steakhouse', 'Sushi', 'Tacos', 'Thai', 'Ukrainian', 'Vegan/Vegetarian', 'Vietnamese', 'Wine', 'Wings']
            };
            window.skipthedishes.RestaurantInputFilter.init(restaurantInputFilterParams);

            var restaurantSortParams = {
                filterInputSelector: '.restaurant-sort-menu',
                callback: function (value) {
                    window.skipthedishes.Loading.showLoading(true);
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        window.skipthedishes.RestaurantSearch.sortFilter(value);
                        window.skipthedishes.RestaurantSearch.updateRestaurantList();
                    }, 0);
                },
                eventHandler: filterEventHandler,
                subscribeEventName: 'mobileSortChanged',
                publishEventName: 'mobileSortChanged',
                activeMenuItemClass: 'menu-item-action',
                regularMenuItemClass: 'menu-item-link',
                disabledMenuItemClass: 'menu-item-disabled',
                sortSelectorAreaSelector: '.sort-selector',
                sortMenuSelector: '.sort-menu',
                sortCaptionSelector: ".sort-caption",
                sortClearSelector: ".sort-clear-x",
                defaultSortValue: 'DEFAULT'
            };
            window.skipthedishes.RestaurantSort.init(restaurantSortParams);

            var mobileHelperMessageParams = {
                helperMessageSelector: "#mobile-helper-message-top",
                helperMessageBodySelector: "#mobile-helper-message-body",
                overlaySelector: "#main-content",
                overlayClass: 'pulse-message-overlay'
            };
            window.skipthedishes.MobileHelperMessage.init(mobileHelperMessageParams);

            var copyToClipboardParams = {
                clipboardSelector: '.clipboard-copy',
                targetName: 'Voucher'
            };
            window.skipthedishes.CopyToClipboard.init(copyToClipboardParams);
        });
    </script>
